  2994. # [21:28] <derf> Let me back up and explain what is going on here, because I think it is not clear to you.
  2995. # [21:28] <derf> libvpx has a number of C structs which are used from the asm.
  2996. # [21:29] <derf> In order to make sure it gets the offsets to the structure members right, it tries to extract them from what the C compiler thinks they are.
  2997. # [21:29] <derf> There are two ways of doing that.
  2998. # [21:29] <glandium> ah, got it
  2999. # [21:29] <derf> One is to build an object file that has a constant value in it for each offset, and the parse the object file.
  3000. # [21:30] * Quits: gmoro (guilherme@84484EC9.1F1093E8.D159334F.IP) (Client exited)

  3002. # [21:30] <derf> That's the VPX_NEED_OBJ_INT_EXTRACT, and the one that is failing on alder.
  3003. # [21:30] <derf> The other is to use gcc inline asm to declare some constants, and grep them out of the generated .s file.
  3004. # [21:30] * bear is now known as bear-afk
